# üõ† Tech Stack

### **Backend**
- Java 17  
- Spring Boot 3.5.x  
- Spring MVC  
- Spring Data JPA  
- Spring Security  
- Spring Validation  
- Actuator  
- Flyway Migration  
- Lombok  

### **Frontend**
- Thymeleaf  
- HTML5 / CSS3 / JS  
- Bootstrap 5  
- Chart.js  

### **Database**
- PostgreSQL 15  
- Docker + docker-compose  
- pgAdmin4  

### **Dev / Tools**
- IntelliJ IDEA  
- VS Code
- Maven  
- Git + GitLab  
- Docker Desktop

# üß± Installation & Setup

## 1Ô∏è‚É£ Clone Repository  
```bash
git clone https://gitlab.com/YOUR_REPO_HERE/finplanpro.git
cd finplanpro

2Ô∏è‚É£ Run PostgreSQL + pgAdmin (Docker)
docker-compose up -d

pgAdmin available at:
 ‚û° http://localhost:5050
 Login:
Email: admin@finplanpro.com
Password: admin123


Database info:
Host: finplanpro-db
Port: 5432
DB: finplanpro
User: postgres
Pass: postgres



3Ô∏è‚É£ Configure application.yml
(‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå‡πÉ‡∏ô‡πÇ‡∏õ‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πå‡∏°‡∏µ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß)

  datasource:
    url: jdbc:postgresql://finplanpro-db:5432/finplanpro
    username: postgres
    password: postgres


4Ô∏è‚É£ Run Migration (Flyway)
‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î Spring Boot ‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß Flyway ‡∏à‡∏∞ migrate ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡πÇ‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥

‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏™‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏à ‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏´‡πá‡∏ô log:

5Ô∏è‚É£ Access Application
http://localhost:8080

D2.2 Feature Description : ‡∏ü‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Å‡πå‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ß‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÇ‡∏õ‡∏£‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå‡∏™‡πà‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡πÑ‡∏ß‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ ‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡∏î‡∏π‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏î‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡πÑ‡∏ß‡πâ (‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠, ‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏™‡∏Å‡∏∏‡∏•, ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏®, ‡∏õ‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏î, ‡∏≠‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏•, ‡∏£‡∏´‡∏±‡∏™‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô), ‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ç‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏à‡∏à‡∏∏‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô, ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏•‡∏ö‡πÇ‡∏õ‡∏£‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ

D2.2 User Journey : 
‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏ô‡∏π "üë§‡πÇ‡∏õ‡∏£‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå"
‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ç‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•:
‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÜ (‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠, ‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏™‡∏Å‡∏∏‡∏•, ‡∏≠‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏• ‡∏Ø‡∏•‡∏Ø) ‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏ä‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ç‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ
‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ç‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á ‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏Å‡∏î‡∏õ‡∏∏‡πà‡∏° "Save Changes" ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ
‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏≠‡πÇ‡∏õ‡∏£‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÅ‡∏à‡πâ‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ô
‡∏•‡∏ö‡πÇ‡∏õ‡∏£‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå:
‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏•‡∏ö‡πÇ‡∏õ‡∏£‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ (‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏°‡∏±‡∏î‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏á) ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏Å‡∏î‡∏õ‡∏∏‡πà‡∏° "Delete Profile" ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏∑‡∏ô‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á ‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏∑‡∏ô‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏ô ‡πÇ‡∏õ‡∏£‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå‡∏Å‡πá‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö
‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏£‡πá‡∏à ‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏≠‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡πà‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÇ‡∏õ‡∏£‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå‡∏≠‡∏∑‡πà‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠ ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏ô‡∏π‡∏≠‡∏∑‡πà‡∏ô‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏î‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏ã‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ
D2.2 ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏≠‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÇ‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏î python :
	‡∏Ñ‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏™ ProfileManagement ‡∏™‡∏∑‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏≠‡∏î‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Frame
‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏ò‡∏≠‡∏î setup_ui: ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏ò‡∏≠‡∏î‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏≠‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ü‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Å‡πå‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏•‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏¥‡∏° (clear_page), ‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡∏´‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠, ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏™‡πà‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏≤ (Search) ‡∏ã‡∏∂‡πà‡∏á‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ Label, Entry ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏Å Username, ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ Button "Search" ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏î‡∏õ‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏≤ ‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏ò‡∏≠‡∏î search_user
‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏ò‡∏≠‡∏î search_user: ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Username ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏ä‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏≤ ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏ô‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏• (get_connection) ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏á users ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏™‡∏±‡πà‡∏á SELECT ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ WHERE username LIKE ? (‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏™‡πà‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ) ‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏û‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏• ‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏Å display_user_profile ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡∏ú‡∏• ‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏û‡∏ö ‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á messagebox.showerror
‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏ò‡∏≠‡∏î display_user_profile: ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏û‡∏ö (‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô tuple) ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á Label ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ Entry ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏™‡πà‡∏ß‡∏ô (Username, Password (‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô '*'), First Name, Last Name, Gender, Year of Birth, Email) ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏°‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏•‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ô Entry ‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏ä‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏õ‡∏∏‡πà‡∏° "Save Changes" (‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏Å save_updated_profile) ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ "Delete Profile" (‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏Å delete_user_profile)
‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏ò‡∏≠‡∏î save_updated_profile: ‡∏î‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ç‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Entry ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏ä‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏ö‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏™‡∏±‡πà‡∏á UPDATE ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏õ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏ï‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏á users ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡∏≠‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏≠‡∏¥‡∏á‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Username ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏¥‡∏° (self.username ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏Å‡πá‡∏ö‡πÑ‡∏ß‡πâ‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡∏ú‡∏•) ‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏à ‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á messagebox.showinfo ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏≤ (setup_ui)
‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏ò‡∏≠‡∏î delete_user_profile: ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Username ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏•‡∏ö ‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á messagebox.askyesno ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏∑‡∏ô‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏•‡∏ö ‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏¢‡∏∑‡∏ô‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏ô ‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏™‡∏±‡πà‡∏á DELETE ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏•‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏á users ‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏à ‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á messagebox.showinfo ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏≤ (setup_ui)
‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏ò‡∏≠‡∏î clear_page: ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏ü‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Å‡πå‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ß‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏•‡∏ö widget ‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ô self.container ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏°‡∏û‡∏∑‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà
D2.2 ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÇ‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏î python ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô Web Spring boots :
	class ProfileManagement(Frame):
    """Class for managing user profiles."""
    def __init__(self, master):
        super().__init__(master, bg="white")
        self.master = master
        self.container = Frame(self, bg="white")
        self.container.pack(fill="both", expand=True)
        self.setup_ui()


    def clear_page(self):
        """Clear all widgets in the current page."""
        for widget in self.container.winfo_children():
            widget.destroy()


        # ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤ container ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô
        if hasattr(self, 'container'):
            for widget in self.container.winfo_children():
                widget.destroy()
        else:
            messagebox.showerror("‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏û‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏î", "‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏û‡∏ö Widget container")




    def setup_ui(self):
        """Setup the profile management UI."""
        if hasattr(self, 'login_frame'):
            self.login_frame.destroy()
            self.login_screen()


        self.clear_page()  # ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏Å‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ clear_page() ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏•‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô
        Label(self.container, text="‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÇ‡∏õ‡∏£‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå (Profile Management)", fg='black', bg='white', font=('arial', 16, 'bold')).pack(pady=20) # Updated font and color


        search_frame = Frame(self.container, bg="white")
        search_frame.pack(fill="both", expand=True, pady=10)


        Label(search_frame, text="‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏Å Uername ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ç‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏• :", bg="white", font=("arial", 14, "bold")).pack(side="top", padx=5, pady=5) # Updated font
        search_entry = Entry(search_frame, font=("arial", 14)) # Updated font
        search_entry.pack(side="top", padx=5, pady=5)


        Button(search_frame, text="üîçSearch", command=lambda: self.search_user(search_entry.get()), font=("arial", 12, "bold"), bg="#4c00ff", fg="white").pack(side="top", padx=5, pady=10) # Updated font and color


        self.user_info_frame = Frame(self.container, bg="white")
        self.user_info_frame.pack(fill="both", expand=True, pady=10)


    def search_user(self, username):
        """Search for a user and show their profile information."""
        if not username:
            messagebox.showwarning("‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏ö‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏ô", "‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏≤")
            return


        conn = get_connection()
        cursor = conn.cursor()


        cursor.execute("SELECT * FROM users WHERE username LIKE ?", ('%' + username + '%',))
        user_data = cursor.fetchone()
        conn.close()


        if user_data:
            self.display_user_profile(user_data)
        else:
            messagebox.showerror("‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏û‡∏ö‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ", "‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏û‡∏ö‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ")


    def display_user_profile(self, user_data):
        """Display the profile of the searched user."""
          # ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏Å‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ clear_page() ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏•‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà


        # ‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ
        self.username = user_data[5]
        self.password = user_data[6]
        self.first_name = user_data[1]
        self.last_name = user_data[2]
        self.gender = user_data[3]
        self.year_of_birth = user_data[4]
        self.email = user_data[0]


        # ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á UI ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•
        Label(self.user_info_frame, text="Username: ", bg="white", font=("arial", 14, "bold")).pack(pady=5)
        self.username_entry = Entry(self.user_info_frame, bg="white", fg="black", font=("arial", 14),width=25)
        self.username_entry.insert(0, self.username)
        self.username_entry.pack(pady=5)


        Label(self.user_info_frame, text="Password: ", bg="white", font=("arial", 14, "bold")).pack(pady=5)
        self.password_entry = Entry(self.user_info_frame, bg="white", fg="black", show="*", font=("arial", 14),width=25)
        self.password_entry.insert(0, self.password)
        self.password_entry.pack(pady=5)


        Label(self.user_info_frame, text="First Name: ", bg="white", font=("arial", 14, "bold")).pack(pady=5)
        self.first_name_entry = Entry(self.user_info_frame, bg="white", fg="black", font=("arial", 14),width=25)
        self.first_name_entry.insert(0, self.first_name)
        self.first_name_entry.pack(pady=5)


        Label(self.user_info_frame, text="Last Name: ", bg="white", font=("arial", 14, "bold")).pack(pady=5)
        self.last_name_entry = Entry(self.user_info_frame, bg="white", fg="black", font=("arial", 14),width=25)
        self.last_name_entry.insert(0, self.last_name)
        self.last_name_entry.pack(pady=5)


        Label(self.user_info_frame, text="Gender: ", bg="white", font=("arial", 14, "bold")).pack(pady=5)
        self.gender_entry = Entry(self.user_info_frame, bg="white", fg="black", font=("arial", 14),width=25)
        self.gender_entry.insert(0, self.gender)
        self.gender_entry.pack(pady=5)


        Label(self.user_info_frame, text="Year of Birth: ", bg="white", font=("arial", 14, "bold")).pack(pady=5)
        self.year_of_birth_entry = Entry(self.user_info_frame, bg="white", fg="black", font=("arial", 14),width=25)
        self.year_of_birth_entry.insert(0, self.year_of_birth)
        self.year_of_birth_entry.pack(pady=5)


        Label(self.user_info_frame, text="Email: ", bg="white", font=("arial", 14, "bold")).pack(pady=5)
        self.email_entry = Entry(self.user_info_frame, bg="white", fg="black", font=("arial", 14),width=25)
        self.email_entry.insert(0, self.email)
        self.email_entry.pack(pady=5)


        # Save button to update the data
        self.save_button = Button(self.user_info_frame, text="Save Changes", font=("arial", 14, "bold"), bg="#4c00ff", fg="white", command=lambda: self.save_updated_profile()) # Updated font and color
        self.save_button.pack(pady=5,padx=20,side="right")


        # Delete button
        self.delete_button = Button(self.user_info_frame, text="Delete Profile", font=("arial", 14, "bold"), bg="#FF4C4C", fg="white", command=lambda: self.delete_user_profile(self.username)) # Updated font and color (using red for delete)
        self.delete_button.pack(pady=5,padx=20,side="right")


    def save_updated_profile(self):
        """Save the updated profile information to the database."""
        new_username = self.username_entry.get()
        new_password = self.password_entry.get()
        new_first_name = self.first_name_entry.get()
        new_last_name = self.last_name_entry.get()
        new_gender = self.gender_entry.get()
        new_year_of_birth = self.year_of_birth_entry.get()
        new_email = self.email_entry.get()


        if not all([new_username, new_password, new_first_name, new_last_name, new_gender, new_year_of_birth, new_email]):
            messagebox.showerror("‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏ö‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏ô", "‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏ä‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á")
            return


        conn = get_connection()
        cursor = conn.cursor()


        cursor.execute("""
            UPDATE users
            SET username = ?, password = ?, first_name = ?, last_name = ?, gender = ?, year = ?, email_id = ?
            WHERE username = ?
        """, (new_username, new_password, new_first_name, new_last_name, new_gender, new_year_of_birth, new_email, self.username))
        conn.commit()
        conn.close()


        messagebox.showinfo("‡∏™‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏à", "‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏õ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏ï‡πÇ‡∏õ‡∏£‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ö‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß!")
        self.setup_ui()


    def delete_user_profile(self, username):
        """Delete a user's profile."""
        if messagebox.askyesno("‡∏¢‡∏∑‡∏ô‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏•‡∏ö", "‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì‡πÅ‡∏ô‡πà‡πÉ‡∏à‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏•‡∏ö‡πÇ‡∏õ‡∏£‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ?"):
            conn = get_connection()
            cursor = conn.cursor()
            cursor.execute("DELETE FROM users WHERE username=?", (username,))
            conn.commit()
            conn.close()


            messagebox.showinfo("‡∏™‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏à", "‡∏•‡∏ö‡πÇ‡∏õ‡∏£‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ö‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß!")
            self.setup_ui()

D3 Feature Description : ‡∏ü‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Å‡πå‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ß‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏¥‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì ‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏™‡πà‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏à‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô ‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏∏‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏à‡∏à‡∏∏‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô, ‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏∏‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏≤‡∏î‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì, ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏à‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏à‡∏à‡∏∏‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô, ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏¥‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏ü‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏≤‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ì‡πå, ‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏∏‡∏Ç‡∏±‡∏¢‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏≤‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ì‡πå, ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏≤‡∏î‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏•‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏ô‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ì‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏à‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÅ‡∏ó‡πâ‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á ‡∏ì ‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì (‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏¥‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏ü‡πâ‡∏≠), ‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ ‡∏ì ‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏à‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏∏‡∏Ç‡∏±‡∏¢‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏≤‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ì‡πå, ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏•‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏°‡πà‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏£‡∏•‡∏∏‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô ‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏î‡∏π‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏¢‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡πÑ‡∏ß‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ

D3 User Journey : 
	‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏ô‡∏π "üè°‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì"
‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ü‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡∏°‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô:
‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏´‡πá‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏à‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô ‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏∏‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏à‡∏à‡∏∏‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô, ‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏∏‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì, ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏à‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏à‡∏à‡∏∏‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô, ‡∏Ñ‡∏≤‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ì‡πå‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏¥‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏ü‡πâ‡∏≠, ‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏∏‡∏Ç‡∏±‡∏¢‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏≤‡∏î‡∏´‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏á, ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏•‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì
‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ì‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô:
‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß ‡∏Å‡∏î‡∏õ‡∏∏‡πà‡∏° "‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ì‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏à‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì"
‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏• ‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á ‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ì‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏•‡∏±‡∏û‡∏ò‡πå‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏´‡πá‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏î‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏à‡∏≠ ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô:
‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏à‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏õ‡∏µ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á‡πÜ ‡∏ì ‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì (‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏¥‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏ü‡πâ‡∏≠‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß)
‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏Å‡πá‡∏ö‡πÑ‡∏ß‡πâ ‡∏ì ‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏û‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏à‡∏ô‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏∏‡∏Ç‡∏±‡∏¢
‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏°‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏Å‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ô‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏•‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏ó‡πà‡∏≤‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏£‡πà‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ
‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô:
‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏û‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏à‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ ‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡∏Å‡∏î‡∏õ‡∏∏‡πà‡∏° "‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì" ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏Å‡πá‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏ß‡πâ‡∏î‡∏π‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ
‡∏î‡∏π‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô:
‡∏Å‡∏î‡∏õ‡∏∏‡πà‡∏° "‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô" ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏î‡∏π‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏¢‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡πÑ‡∏ß‡πâ
‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ ‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ "‡∏•‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î" ‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ
‡∏Å‡∏î "‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏ü‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡∏°" ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô

D3 ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏≠‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÇ‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏î python :
	‡∏Ñ‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏™ RetirementForm ‡∏™‡∏∑‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏≠‡∏î‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å BaseForm
‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏ò‡∏≠‡∏î setup_form_view: ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á Frame ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å, ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á StringVar ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏Å‡πá‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏• input ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÜ, ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á Label, Entry, ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ Spinbox ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏• (‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô ‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏∏‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏à‡∏à‡∏∏‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô, ‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏∏‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì, ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏à‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢), ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏õ‡∏∏‡πà‡∏° "‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ì‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏à‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì", "‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì", ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ "‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô", ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á Frame ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏•‡∏±‡∏û‡∏ò‡πå‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ì (self.result_label_annual_expense, self.result_label_total_needed, self.result_label_monthly_investment)
‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏ò‡∏≠‡∏î calculate_retirement: ‡∏î‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å StringVar, ‡πÅ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏Ç (int/float) ‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏î‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏à‡∏±‡∏ö ValueError, ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ì‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏õ‡∏µ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏õ‡∏µ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì, ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ì‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏à‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ô ‡∏ì ‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏¥‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏ü‡πâ‡∏≠ (Future Value), ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ì‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏à‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏õ‡∏µ‡πÅ‡∏£‡∏Å ‡∏ì ‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì, ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ì "‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÅ‡∏ó‡πâ‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì" (Real Rate of Return) ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏¥‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏ü‡πâ‡∏≠, ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ì "‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ ‡∏ì ‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì" ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏™‡∏π‡∏ï‡∏£ Present Value of Annuity ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏à‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏õ‡∏µ‡πÅ‡∏£‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÅ‡∏ó‡πâ‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì, ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ì "‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏•‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì" ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏™‡∏π‡∏ï‡∏£ Future Value of Ordinary Annuity ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤ PMT (Periodic Payment) ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏Å‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢ (total_investment_needed) ‡∏ì ‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì ‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏ì‡∏µ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏®‡∏© ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô 0 ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏•‡∏ö‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏Å ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏î‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏à‡∏±‡∏ö OverflowError ‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏•‡∏±‡∏û‡∏ò‡πå‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏õ, ‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏ó‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏¢ ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏õ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏ï‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏ô Label ‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏•‡∏±‡∏û‡∏ò‡πå (.config())
‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏ò‡∏≠‡∏î save: ‡∏î‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏• input, ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ì total_investment_needed ‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á (‡∏Ñ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏¢ calculate_retirement ‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡πÄ‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏™‡πà‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏à‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å), ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•, ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏™‡∏±‡πà‡∏á INSERT ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏• input ‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ total_investment_needed ‡∏•‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏á retirement
‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏ò‡∏≠‡∏î show_list_view: ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏∏‡∏°‡∏°‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡∏ã‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô Frame ‡∏ü‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡∏° ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏Å setup_list_view
‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏ò‡∏≠‡∏î setup_list_view: ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á Frame ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£, ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ SELECT ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏á retirement, ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á ttk.Treeview ‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏° Scrollbar, ‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î‡∏Ñ‡∏≠‡∏•‡∏±‡∏°‡∏ô‡πå‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏´‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠, ‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏°‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏•‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ô Treeview ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏£‡∏π‡∏õ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏Ç, ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏õ‡∏∏‡πà‡∏° "‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏ü‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡∏°" ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ "‡∏•‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î"
‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏ò‡∏≠‡∏î back_to_form: ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏∏‡∏°‡∏°‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÑ‡∏õ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏ü‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡∏°
‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏ò‡∏≠‡∏î delete_all_retirement: ‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á messagebox.askyesno ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏∑‡∏ô‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏ô, ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏™‡∏±‡πà‡∏á DELETE ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏•‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏á retirement, ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÇ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏î‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÉ‡∏ô Treeview ‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà

D3 ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÇ‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏î python ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô Web Spring boots :
	class RetirementForm(BaseForm):
    """Retirement form class."""
    def __init__(self, master):
        super().__init__(master, "‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì (Retirement Planning)")
        self.current_view = "form"
        self.setup_form_view()
        self.retirement_data = []


    def setup_form_view(self):
        """Set up the form view for retirement planning."""
        self.form_frame = tk.Frame(self, bg="white")
        self.form_frame.pack(fill="both", expand=True, padx=20, pady=10)


        self.age = tk.StringVar()
        self.retirement_age_var = tk.StringVar(value=60)
        self.monthly_expense = tk.StringVar()
        self.inflation_rate = tk.StringVar(value=3)
        self.life_expectancy = tk.StringVar(value=90)
        self.pre_retirement_return = tk.StringVar(value=8)
        self.post_retirement_return = tk.StringVar(value=3)


     
        columns_frame = tk.Frame(self.form_frame, bg="white")
        columns_frame.pack(fill="both", pady=10,padx=50)


        left_column = tk.Frame(columns_frame, bg="white")
        left_column.pack(side="left", fill="x", expand=True, padx=20)


        right_column = tk.Frame(columns_frame, bg="white")
        right_column.pack(side="right", fill="x", expand=True)
     
        tk.Label(left_column, text="‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏∏‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏à‡∏à‡∏∏‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô:", bg="white", font=("arial", 14, "bold")).pack(anchor="e", pady=15)
        tk.Entry(right_column, textvariable=self.age, font=("arial", 14),width=20).pack(anchor="w",pady=15)


        tk.Label(left_column, text="‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏∏‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì:", bg="white", font=("arial", 14, "bold")).pack(anchor="e", pady=15)
        tk.Spinbox(right_column, textvariable=self.retirement_age_var, from_=0, to=120,  font=("arial", 14),width=20).pack(anchor="w",pady=15) # Use renamed variable


        tk.Label(left_column, text="‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏à‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ô (THB):", bg="white", font=("arial", 14, "bold")).pack(anchor="e", pady=15)
        tk.Entry(right_column, textvariable=self.monthly_expense,  font=("arial", 14),width=20).pack(anchor="w",pady=15)


        tk.Label(left_column, text="‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏¥‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏ü‡πâ‡∏≠ (%):", bg="white", font=("arial", 14, "bold")).pack(anchor="e", pady=15)
        tk.Spinbox(right_column, textvariable=self.inflation_rate,from_=1, to=10, font=("arial", 14),width=20).pack(anchor="w",pady=15)


        tk.Label(left_column, text="‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏∏‡∏Ç‡∏±‡∏¢‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏≤‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ì‡πå:", bg="white", font=("arial", 14, "bold")).pack(anchor="e", pady=15)
        tk.Spinbox(right_column, textvariable=self.life_expectancy,from_=0, to=120,  font=("arial", 14),width=20).pack(anchor="w",pady=15)


        tk.Label(left_column, text="‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏•‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏ô (‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì) (%):", bg="white", font=("arial", 14, "bold")).pack(anchor="e", pady=15)
        tk.Spinbox(right_column, textvariable=self.pre_retirement_return,from_=0, to=30,  font=("arial", 14),width=20).pack(anchor="w",pady=15)


        tk.Label(left_column, text="‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏•‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏ô (‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì) (%):", bg="white", font=("arial", 14, "bold")).pack(anchor="e", pady=15)
        tk.Spinbox(right_column, textvariable=self.post_retirement_return,from_=0, to=30,  font=("arial", 14),width=20).pack(anchor="w",pady=15)
        # --- End Placement ---


        button_frame = tk.Frame(self.form_frame, bg="white")
        button_frame.pack(pady=10)


        tk.Button(button_frame, text="‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ì‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏à‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì", command=self.calculate_retirement,bg="#4c00ff",fg="white",font=("arial",14,"bold")).pack(side="left", padx=10)
        tk.Button(button_frame, text="‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì", command=self.save,bg="white",font=("arial",14,"bold")).pack(side="left", padx=10)
     
        tk.Button(button_frame, text="‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô", command=self.show_list_view, font=("arial", 14, "bold")).pack(side="left", padx=10)
       
   
        self.bottom_frame = tk.Frame(self.form_frame, bg="#4c00ff")
        self.bottom_frame.pack(side="bottom", fill="both", expand=True, padx=200, pady=50)
        self.result_label_annual_expense = tk.Label(self.bottom_frame, text="‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏à‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏õ‡∏µ‡πÅ‡∏£‡∏Å ‡∏ì ‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì (‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏õ‡∏µ): 0.00 ", bg="#4c00ff", font=("arial", 14,"bold"), fg="white", pady=10)
        self.result_label_total_needed = tk.Label(self.bottom_frame, text="‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ ‡∏ì ‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì (THB): 0.00 ", bg="#4c00ff", font=("arial", 14,"bold"), fg="white", pady=10)
        self.result_label_monthly_investment = tk.Label(self.bottom_frame, text="‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏•‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì (THB): 0.00", bg="#4c00ff", font=("arial", 14,"bold"), fg="white", pady=10)
       
        self.result_label_annual_expense.pack(pady=2)
        self.result_label_total_needed.pack(pady=2)
        self.result_label_monthly_investment.pack(pady=2)


    def calculate_retirement(self):
        """Calculates retirement costs and investment requirements."""
        try:
            current_age = int(self.age.get())
            retirement_age = int(self.retirement_age_var.get())
            monthly_expense = float(self.monthly_expense.get())
            inflation_rate = float(self.inflation_rate.get()) / 100
            life_expectancy = int(self.life_expectancy.get())
            pre_retirement_return = float(self.pre_retirement_return.get()) / 100
            post_retirement_return = float(self.post_retirement_return.get()) / 100


            retirement_years = life_expectancy - retirement_age
            years_until_retirement = retirement_age - current_age


            if retirement_years <= 0 or years_until_retirement <= 0:
                messagebox.showerror("‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏û‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏î", "‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏∏‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á (‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏∏‡∏Ç‡∏±‡∏¢‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏∏‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏∏‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏∏‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏à‡∏à‡∏∏‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô)")
                return


            adjusted_monthly_expense = monthly_expense * ((1 + inflation_rate) ** years_until_retirement)
            first_year_annual_expense = adjusted_monthly_expense * 12


     
            if (1 + inflation_rate) == 0:
                 messagebox.showerror("‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏û‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏î", "‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏¥‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏ü‡πâ‡∏≠‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô -100% ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ")
                 return
           
            if (1 + post_retirement_return) == 0 and (1 + inflation_rate) != 0:
                 real_rate_post_retirement = -1.0
            elif (1 + inflation_rate) == 0:
                 real_rate_post_retirement = post_retirement_return
            else:
                 real_rate_post_retirement = ((1 + post_retirement_return) / (1 + inflation_rate)) - 1




            if real_rate_post_retirement == 0:
           
                total_investment_needed = first_year_annual_expense * retirement_years
            elif real_rate_post_retirement < -1:
               
                 total_investment_needed = float('inf')
            else:
             
             
                if (1 + real_rate_post_retirement) <= 0:
             
                     total_investment_needed = float('inf')
                else:
                    try:
                        pv_factor = (1 - (1 + real_rate_post_retirement)**(-retirement_years)) / real_rate_post_retirement
                        total_investment_needed = first_year_annual_expense * pv_factor
                    except OverflowError:
                     
                         total_investment_needed = float('inf')
                         messagebox.showerror("‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ì‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏û‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏î", "‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏•‡∏±‡∏û‡∏ò‡πå‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ì‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏õ ‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏à‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏õ‡∏µ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô‡πÉ‡∏Å‡∏•‡πâ‡∏®‡∏π‡∏ô‡∏¢‡πå")
                         return




           
            monthly_pre_ret_rate = pre_retirement_return / 12
            total_periods_pre_ret = years_until_retirement * 12


            if total_periods_pre_ret <= 0:
                 required_monthly_investment = float('inf') if total_investment_needed > 0 else 0
            elif monthly_pre_ret_rate == 0:
                 required_monthly_investment = total_investment_needed / total_periods_pre_ret
            else:
           
                 if (1 + monthly_pre_ret_rate) <= 0:
                      required_monthly_investment = float('inf')
                 else:
                    try:
                        fv_factor = (((1 + monthly_pre_ret_rate)**total_periods_pre_ret) - 1) / monthly_pre_ret_rate
                     
                        required_monthly_investment = total_investment_needed / fv_factor if fv_factor != 0 else float('inf')
                    except OverflowError:
                        required_monthly_investment = float('inf') # Result too large
                        messagebox.showerror("‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ì‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏û‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏î", "‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏•‡∏±‡∏û‡∏ò‡πå‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ì‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏õ")
                        return




         
            total_needed_str = f"{total_investment_needed:,.2f}" if total_investment_needed != float('inf') else "‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ì‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ (‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏™‡∏π‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏õ/‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏•‡∏ö‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏Å)"
            monthly_inv_str = f"{required_monthly_investment:,.2f}" if required_monthly_investment != float('inf') else "‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ì‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ (‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏™‡∏π‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏õ/‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏û‡∏≠/‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏•‡∏ö‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏Å)"


         
            self.result_label_annual_expense.config(text=f"‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏à‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏õ‡∏µ‡πÅ‡∏£‡∏Å ‡∏ì ‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì (THB): {first_year_annual_expense:,.2f}")
            self.result_label_total_needed.config(text=f"‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ ‡∏ì ‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì (THB): {total_needed_str}")
            self.result_label_monthly_investment.config(text=f"‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏•‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ô ‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì (THB): {monthly_inv_str}")




        except ValueError:
            messagebox.showerror("‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏û‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏î", "‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏Ç‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á")
        except Exception as e:
             messagebox.showerror("‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏û‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ì", f"‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏û‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏î: {e}")




    def save(self):
        """Saves retirement data (using retirement_age and calculated needed amount)."""
        try:
           
            current_age = int(self.age.get())
            retirement_age = int(self.retirement_age_var.get())
            monthly_expense_val = float(self.monthly_expense.get())
            inflation_rate = float(self.inflation_rate.get()) / 100
            life_expectancy = int(self.life_expectancy.get())
           
            post_retirement_return = float(self.post_retirement_return.get()) / 100


            retirement_years = life_expectancy - retirement_age
            years_until_retirement = retirement_age - current_age


            if retirement_years <= 0 or years_until_retirement <= 0:
                messagebox.showerror("‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏û‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏î", "‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏∏‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ")
                return


            adjusted_monthly_expense = monthly_expense_val * ((1 + inflation_rate) ** years_until_retirement)
            first_year_annual_expense = adjusted_monthly_expense * 12


            if (1 + inflation_rate) == 0:
                 messagebox.showerror("‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏û‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏î", "‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏¥‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏ü‡πâ‡∏≠‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ")
                 return
            if (1 + post_retirement_return) == 0 and (1 + inflation_rate) != 0:
                 real_rate_post_retirement = -1.0
            elif (1 + inflation_rate) == 0:
                 real_rate_post_retirement = post_retirement_return
            else:
                 real_rate_post_retirement = ((1 + post_retirement_return) / (1 + inflation_rate)) - 1


            if real_rate_post_retirement == 0:
                total_investment_needed = first_year_annual_expense * retirement_years
            elif real_rate_post_retirement < -1 or (1 + real_rate_post_retirement) <= 0:
                 total_investment_needed = float('inf')
            else:
                try:
                    pv_factor = (1 - (1 + real_rate_post_retirement)**(-retirement_years)) / real_rate_post_retirement
                    total_investment_needed = first_year_annual_expense * pv_factor
                except (OverflowError, ZeroDivisionError):
                     total_investment_needed = float('inf')


            if total_investment_needed == float('inf'):
                 messagebox.showerror("‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏û‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏î", "‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ì‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å")
                 return


         
            conn = get_connection()
            cursor = conn.cursor()
         
            cursor.execute("""
                INSERT INTO retirement (
                    current_age, retirement_age, monthly_expense, inflation_rate,
                    life_expectancy, pre_retirement_return, post_retirement_return, target_money
                ) VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
            """, (
                current_age, retirement_age, monthly_expense_val,
                float(self.inflation_rate.get()),
                life_expectancy,
                float(self.pre_retirement_return.get()),
                float(self.post_retirement_return.get()),
                total_investment_needed
            ))
            conn.commit()
            self.confirm("‚úÖ ‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß")
     


        except ValueError:
            messagebox.showerror("‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏û‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏î", "‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏Ç‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å")
        except sqlite3.Error as e:
            messagebox.showerror("Database Error", f"‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ: {e}")
            if conn:
                conn.rollback()
        except Exception as e:
             messagebox.showerror("‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏û‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏î", f"‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏û‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å: {e}")
        finally:
            if conn:
                conn.close()


    def show_list_view(self):
        """Show list of retirement plans."""
 
        if hasattr(self, 'form_frame') and self.form_frame.winfo_exists():
            self.form_frame.pack_forget()
     
        if hasattr(self, 'list_frame') and self.list_frame.winfo_exists():
            self.list_frame.destroy()


        self.current_view = "list"
        self.title_label.config(text="‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì")
        self.setup_list_view()


    def setup_list_view(self):
        """Set up the list view for retirement plans."""
        self.list_frame = tk.Frame(self, bg="white")
        self.list_frame.pack(fill="both", expand=True)


       
        conn = get_connection()
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        try:
         
            cursor.execute("""
                SELECT id, current_age, retirement_age, monthly_expense,
                       inflation_rate, life_expectancy, pre_retirement_return,
                       post_retirement_return, target_money
                FROM retirement
            """)
            self.retirement_data = cursor.fetchall()
        except sqlite3.Error as e:
            messagebox.showerror("Database Error", f"‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡πÇ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏î‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ: {e}")
            self.retirement_data = []
        finally:
            conn.close()


        if not self.retirement_data:
            tk.Label(self.list_frame, text="‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì", bg="white", font=("arial", 14)).pack(pady=20)
        else:
            # --- Treeview Setup ---
            tree_frame = tk.Frame(self.list_frame)
            tree_frame.pack(fill="both", expand=True, padx=10, pady=10)


            # Scrollbars
            vsb = ttk.Scrollbar(tree_frame, orient="vertical")
            vsb.pack(side='right', fill='y')
            hsb = ttk.Scrollbar(tree_frame, orient="horizontal")
            hsb.pack(side='bottom', fill='x')


            # --- Define all columns for Treeview ---
            column_ids = ("id", "current_age", "retirement_age", "monthly_expense",
                          "inflation", "life_expectancy", "pre_ret_return",
                          "post_ret_return", "target_money")
            column_headings = ("ID", "‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏∏ ‡∏õ‡∏à‡∏ö.", "‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏∏‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì", "‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏à‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢/‡∏î",
                               "‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏¥‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏ü‡πâ‡∏≠(%)", "‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏∏‡∏Ç‡∏±‡∏¢", "‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô(%)",
                               "‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á(%)", "‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ(THB)")


            retirement_tree = ttk.Treeview(tree_frame, columns=column_ids, show="headings",
                                           yscrollcommand=vsb.set, xscrollcommand=hsb.set)
            vsb.config(command=retirement_tree.yview)
            hsb.config(command=retirement_tree.xview)


            # --- Configure headings and columns ---
            for col_id, heading in zip(column_ids, column_headings):
                retirement_tree.heading(col_id, text=heading)
                width = 80 # Default width
                anchor = "center"
                if col_id == "id":
                    width = 40
                elif col_id == "target_money":
                    width = 150
                    anchor = "e"
                elif col_id == "monthly_expense":
                    width = 100
                    anchor = "e"
                retirement_tree.column(col_id, width=width, anchor=anchor)


            # --- Insert data into Treeview ---
            for plan in self.retirement_data:
                # Format numerical data for display
                formatted_values = list(plan) # Convert tuple to list for modification
                formatted_values[3] = f"{plan[3]:,.2f}" # monthly_expense
                formatted_values[8] = f"{plan[8]:,.2f}" # target_money
                retirement_tree.insert("", "end", values=(
                    tuple(formatted_values) # Convert back to tuple
                ))


            retirement_tree.pack(fill="both", expand=True)
            # --- End Treeview Setup ---


        # --- Button Frame ---
        button_frame = tk.Frame(self.list_frame, bg="white")
        button_frame.pack(pady=10)


        tk.Button(button_frame, text="‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏ü‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡∏°", command=self.back_to_form, font=("arial", 14, "bold")).pack(side="left", padx=10)
        if self.retirement_data:
            tk.Button(button_frame, text="‡∏•‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î", command=self.delete_all_retirement, font=("arial", 14, "bold"), fg="red").pack(side="left", padx=10)


    def back_to_form(self):
        """Go back to the form view."""


        if hasattr(self, 'list_frame') and self.list_frame.winfo_exists():
            self.list_frame.destroy()
       
        if not hasattr(self, 'form_frame') or not self.form_frame.winfo_exists():
             self.setup_form_view()
        else:
             self.form_frame.pack(fill="both", expand=True, padx=20, pady=10)
        self.current_view = "form"
        self.title_label.config(text="‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì")




    def delete_all_retirement(self):
        """Delete all retirement plans."""
        if messagebox.askyesno("‡∏¢‡∏∑‡∏ô‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏ô", "‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏•‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà? ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡∏¢‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ"):
            conn = None
            try:
                conn = get_connection()
                cursor = conn.cursor()
                cursor.execute("DELETE FROM retirement")
                conn.commit()
                self.confirm("‚úÖ ‡∏•‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß")
            except sqlite3.Error as e:
                messagebox.showerror("Database Error", f"‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏û‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏•‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•: {e}")
                if conn:
                    conn.rollback()
            finally:
                if conn:
                    conn.close()
       
                self.show_list_view()



üéØ D4 ‚Äî Retirement Planner (Advanced ‚Äì 7 Steps Duolingo Style)
Branch: feature/D4-retirement-advanced
‡∏≠‡∏¥‡∏á‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡πÑ‡∏ü‡∏•‡πå V.4 ‚Äî 7 Stages: YOU ‚Üí LIFE ‚Üí WANT ‚Üí HAVES ‚Üí DESIGN ‚Üí TEST ‚Üí SAVE
D4.1 Setup Flow Controller (Step-by-step Wizard)
D4.2 Step 1 (YOU): DOB, Gender, Retire Age
D4.3 Step 2 (LIFE): Health Quiz ‚Üí Predict Life Expectancy
D4.4 Step 3 (WANT): Lifestyle, desired monthly cost
D4.5 Step 4 (EXPENSE): Basic + Special Cost (FV calculation)
D4.6 Step 5 (HAVES): Assets, RMF/SSF, pension, annuity
D4.7 Step 6 (DESIGN): Target Gap Solver
D4.8 Step 7 (TEST): 4 Scenarios Simulation
D4.9 Save retirement plan
D4.10 Visualization Graph (3-layer chart)
D4.11 Commit: Retirement Advanced Completed

D4 Feature Description : 
	‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏• ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ ‡∏™‡∏¥‡πà‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏â‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÉ‡∏ô üéØ D4 ‚Äî Retirement Planner (Advanced ‚Äì 7 Steps Duolingo Style) **

The 7 Steps:
YOU: Display calculated Age. Ask: "At what age do you want to retire?" ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ (‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô)
‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà: ‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î‡∏à‡∏∏‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏™‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏¢
‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏∏: ‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏õ‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏î, ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏® ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ ‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏∏‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì
‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢ : ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏Å 1.‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏õ‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏î 2.‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏® ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ 3.‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏Å‡πá‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏• ‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ì‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏¢‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏Ñ‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠ ‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì
LIFE (Health Quiz): Ask: "How is your health?" (Options: Excellent, Average, Poor).‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ (‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏∏‡∏Ç‡∏±‡∏¢)
Logic: Excellent = Life Expectancy +3 years; Poor = -3 years. Update the Life Expectancy in the User Profile.
‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà: ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏ä‡∏µ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏∏‡πÄ‡∏ó‡πà‡∏≤‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏£‡πà (Life Expectancy) ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏™‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏ï‡∏∏‡∏™‡∏°‡∏ú‡∏•
‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô:
‡∏°‡∏µ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏Ç‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û‡∏á‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÜ (Excellent, Average, Poor)
‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏∏‡∏Ç‡∏±‡∏¢‡∏Ñ‡∏≤‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ì‡πå (Life Expectancy) ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏•‡∏î‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ô‡∏¢‡∏≥‡∏Ç‡∏∂‡πâ‡∏ô
‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢ :‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ User ‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏ô‡∏≥ ‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏Ç‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ì‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏∏‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏≤‡∏î‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ä‡∏µ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ï
WANTS: Ask: "How much do you spend per month today?" and "Estimated Inflation?" (Default 3%). ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ (‡πÑ‡∏•‡∏ü‡πå‡∏™‡πÑ‡∏ï‡∏•‡πå‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì) 
Logic: Calculate Future Expense = Current Expense * (1.03 ^ YearsToRetire).
‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢ : ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ User ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏¥‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏•‡∏ü‡πå‡∏™‡πÑ‡∏ï‡∏•‡πå‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì ‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏¥‡∏ô ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ì‡πÄ‡∏ó‡πà‡∏≤‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏£‡πà ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏• ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ 1.‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏¢‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏ß‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà 2.‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏° ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà 3.‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏∏‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏û‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏®‡∏©‡∏ô‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô 4.‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏∏‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏¢‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì (‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠) ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ User ‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏•‡∏á‡∏°‡∏≤ ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏à‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢ ‡∏î‡∏±‡∏á‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ 1.‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ ‡∏à‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏õ‡∏Å‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ô 2.‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏à‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏û‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏®‡∏©‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏≤‡∏î‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏Ç‡∏∂‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì 3.‡∏Å‡∏î‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ì‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏°‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤ ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏à‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì (‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏¥‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏ü‡πâ‡∏≠‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß)
HAVES: Ask: "What is your current retirement savings?" (Sum of RMF/LTF + Cash).‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ (‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà)
‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà: ‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏£‡∏±‡∏û‡∏¢‡πå‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏∑‡∏≠
‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô : ‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏£‡∏±‡∏û‡∏¢‡πå‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô ‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πâ‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏ä‡∏µ‡∏û (Provident Fund), ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ö‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏ç, RMF/SSF, ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏û‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡∏ï‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏•‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏∑‡πà‡∏ô‡πÜ
‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ FV Engine ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ì‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏¥‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ ‡∏ì ‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡πÇ‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥
‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢ : ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ User ‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏¥‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏¥‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏à‡∏à‡∏∏‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏£ ‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì‡∏≠‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ö‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏Å 1.‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ ‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì LTF/RMF 2.‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ö‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏ç/‡∏ä‡∏µ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ï 3.‡πÅ‡∏´‡∏•‡πà‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏∑‡πà‡∏ô‡πÜ ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏≠‡∏á ‡∏™‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏Å ‡∏´‡∏∏‡πâ‡∏ô ‡∏≠‡∏™‡∏±‡∏á‡∏´‡∏≤
DESIGN: Ask: "Expected Return on Investment?"‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ (‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö ‡∏û‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡∏ï‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏•‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏à‡∏£‡∏π‡∏õ ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô) 
‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà: ‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏¢‡∏∏‡∏ó‡∏ò‡πå‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏•‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏ô ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ ‡∏û‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡∏ï‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏•‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏à‡∏£‡∏π‡∏õ
‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢ : ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ User ‡πÄ‡∏´‡πá‡∏ô‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏ó‡πà‡∏≤‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏£‡πà ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢ 
‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ì‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏à‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥ ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ô‡∏≥ ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏à‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏°‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì - ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì - ‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß 
‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏ü‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏à‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢ ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏•‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏ô ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏°‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà ‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏Å
‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ì "‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥" ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Ç‡∏≤‡∏î‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà (Gap Analysis)
TEST (Simulation): (‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ì‡πå) 
‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà: ‡∏ó‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÅ‡∏Ç‡πá‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏Å‡∏£‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô (Stress Test)
‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢ : 
‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏•‡∏±‡∏û‡∏ò‡πå‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏¢ 4 Sinario ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ User ‡∏ó‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏ö‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏¥‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ì‡πÄ‡∏ó‡πà‡∏≤‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏£‡πà ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏•‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏ó‡πà‡∏≤‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏£‡πà ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏≤‡∏î‡∏´‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Å‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡πÄ‡∏ã‡πá‡∏ô ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ 
‡∏™‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏õ‡∏™‡∏¥‡πà‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà User ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏°‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô Task ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡∏ô‡∏≥‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏á‡∏°‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ó‡∏≥‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ 
‡∏™‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏õ‡∏™‡∏¥‡πà‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà User ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏û‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏°‡∏±‡∏î‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏á ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏ó‡∏≥‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ ‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏∏‡πà‡∏° Save ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ ‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤ Home  ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ
‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô:
‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ì‡πå‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏¢ 4 Scenarios (‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô ‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏¥‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏ü‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏™‡∏π‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏Ñ‡∏≤‡∏î, ‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≥‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏Ñ‡∏≤‡∏î ‡∏≠‡∏∑‡πà‡∏ô‡πÜ)
‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏à‡∏à‡∏∏‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏ó‡∏≥‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏∏‡πÄ‡∏ó‡πà‡∏≤‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏£‡πà ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏•‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏ó‡πà‡∏≤‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏£‡πà‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏î


Calculate Total Fund Needed using TVM formulas (PV of Annuity).
Calculate Gap = Total Needed - FV of Current Assets.
Calculate PMT = Monthly savings required to fill the gap.
REVIEW (The Result):(‡∏™‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏õ‡∏ú‡∏•)
‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà: ‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏à‡∏á‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢
‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡∏ú‡∏•:
3-Layer Chart: ‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏ü‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡∏ú‡∏• 3 ‡πÄ‡∏™‡πâ‡∏ô ‡∏Ñ‡∏∑‡∏≠ ‡πÄ‡∏™‡πâ‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÉ‡∏™‡πà‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÑ‡∏õ, ‡πÄ‡∏™‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏á‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏¢ ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏™‡πâ‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏õ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á
‡∏™‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏≠‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ (Total Needed) ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏ô‡∏≥ (Monthly Savings Required) ‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏õ‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô
Display a 3-Layer Area Chart (Chart.js):
Layer 1 (Bottom): Principal (Money you save).
Layer 2 (Middle): Growth (Interest earned).
Layer 3 (Line): Target Goal.
Call to Action: "Save Plan" or "Adjust Plan".

	‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏ô‡∏π "üí∞‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏£‡∏±‡∏û‡∏¢‡πå"
‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ü‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡∏°‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å:
‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏´‡πá‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏≠‡πÅ‡∏ö‡πà‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ù‡∏±‡πà‡∏á ‡∏ù‡∏±‡πà‡∏á‡∏ã‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏Å "‡∏ó‡∏£‡∏±‡∏û‡∏¢‡πå‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ô" (‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô ‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏î, ‡∏´‡∏∏‡πâ‡∏ô, ‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏ô, ‡∏ö‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ô, ‡∏£‡∏ñ) ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏ù‡∏±‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ç‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏Å "‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ô" (‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô ‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏î‡∏¥‡∏ï, ‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ö‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ô, ‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏ñ)
‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏õ‡∏∏‡πà‡∏° "‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ì", "‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å" (‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ "‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏õ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏ï" ‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ç), ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ "‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£"
‡∏î‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏™‡πà‡∏ß‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á "‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏°" ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏£‡∏±‡∏û‡∏¢‡πå‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ô, ‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ô, ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏°‡∏±‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡πà‡∏á‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥

‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏£‡∏±‡∏û‡∏¢‡πå‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ô ‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏Å‡∏î‡∏õ‡∏∏‡πà‡∏° "‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ì"

‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å/‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏õ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏ï:

‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà "‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£" ‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤ "‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ç" ‡∏õ‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô "‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏õ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏ï" ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ç‡∏ô‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô

‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£:
